光田康典 YasunoriMitsuda

@YasunoriMitsuda

2021年12月9日

回复 @akio_noguchi

明生ちゃん、今日もお疲れ様でした。今回の作品はとにかくピアノと笛が最も重要だったのですが、どの曲も細かなニュアンスまでしっかりと録音できて本当に良かったし、明生ちゃんにお願いして大正解でした。自分の中で大切な作品になりました。

「アグヌス」は、魔法のような技術「エーテル」に強い国家ですも。軍の構成も、エーテル戦に特化した部隊が中心で、エーテル技術を利用した自立型の小型機動兵器で戦うも。
白っぽくて、エーテル戦が得意なのが「アグヌス」ですも！#ゼノブレイド3 https://t.co/Dbs5JQFwPD<img src="https://p.sda1.dev/4/d39d474a34c066e030028ea53ba9c0e5/IMG_CMP_8630056.jpeg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">
「ケヴェス」は、機械技術が発展した国家ですも。ケヴェス軍は戦闘車をメインとした部隊で構成されていて、人が乗り込んで運用する小型機動兵器の部隊を利用しているそうですも。
とりあえず、服が黒くてメカっぽいのが「ケヴェス」も！#ゼノブレイド3 https://t.co/g7z9pkGEMw<img src="https://p.sda1.dev/4/f6a262220ac5afd06a88cb0a53a3252c/IMG_CMP_27202306.jpeg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

####  godless2020  
##### 415#       发表于 2022-2-10 07:41

《异度神剑 3》所在的世界「艾欧尼翁」，有着两个敌对的国家「凯维斯」和「阿格努斯」，两国间的战争延绵不绝，双方士兵都为了活下去日复一日地战斗。

「凯维斯」是个机械技术发达的国家，部队由"战斗车"为主要构成，士兵携带小型机动兵器战斗，制服为黑色。

「阿格努斯」是个"以太"技术发达的国家，这种技术类似于魔法，军队都是利用以太技术制作的兵器来战斗，制服为白色。

####  stoiorz  
##### 417#       发表于 2022-2-10 07:41

剧情是男女主处各个阵营，男主梅里亚，女主尼亚。战斗中流落荒岛，得育黄药师传授落英缤纷曲子一首，男主习得上阙，女主习得下阙。
而后男主得知女主竟是敌国公主，一番误解与解决之中，两人竟然暗生情愫。
机遇巧合下，女主发出信号最终两个人得救，回到各自阵营。
男主回去后女二问他为何不将彼女除之而后快。男主一番挣扎下道出实情，他想通过其他方式解决两国的资源争夺问题。
没想到女主那边又发生变故，男二过来求援，纠结之中男主决定救出女主，女二亦决定同行。
之后。。。。。我喜欢你还有大家。

—— 来自 [S1Fun](https://s1fun.koalcat.com)

####  seize1121  
##### 442#       发表于 2022-2-10 07:48

高桥访谈

As announced in the latest Nintendo Direct video presentation, the RPG adventure Xenoblade Chronicles 3 is heading to Nintendo Switch this September. To shed some light on this announcement, Executive Director Tetsuya Takahashi shared this message on the upcoming title, including some exciting tidbits that’re sure to be of interest to fans of the series.

Over to you, Mr. Takahashi!

==

Hi everyone, this is Tetsuya Takahashi from MONOLITHSOFT.

Just over four years since the release of Xenoblade Chronicles 2 and one and a half years since the release of Xenoblade Chronicles: Definitive Edition, we now bring to you news regarding the latest game from MONOLITHSOFT: Xenoblade Chronicles 3. As the name indicates, it’s the third installment in the Xenoblade Chronicles series. We are currently making final adjustments to ensure we create the best game possible based on everything we’ve learned from the past entries in the series.

The key visual features a broken great sword of Mechonis and the body of the Urayan Titan with a gaping wound. I imagine everyone who saw the trailer was quite surprised by the final scene. What is this visual hinting at? I can’t reveal that just yet. What I can tell you is that this visual was conceived quite some time ago. More precisely speaking, we came up with it sometime between the end of development of Xenoblade Chronicles and the beginning of development of Xenoblade Chronicles 2. So, it’s not something we recently added to the series.

We believe the game will be enjoyable for both those who’ve played Xenoblade Chronicles or Xenoblade Chronicles 2, as well as those who will be playing a Xenoblade Chronicles game for the first time.

The characters were designed by Masatsugu Saito, who also designed the characters for Xenoblade Chronicles 2. While we can’t reveal them at this time, Koichi Mugitani created some of the game’s key artwork. As you can see, familiar staff members with the Xenoblade Chronicles series have once again come together to create this game.

The game music was also handled by artists who’ve contributed to the series in the past. The music for Xenoblade Chronicles 3 was composed by Yasunori Mitsuda, Manami Kiyota, ACE (TOMOri Kudo, CHiCO), Kenji Hiramatsu and Mariam Abounnasr.

The music in this game maintains the unique Xenoblade Chronicles touch while also taking on a new challenge, namely that of integrating a flute-based melody as its motif. The flute is actually one of the key themes in this game. A variety of other elements and themes are hidden in the trailer andwe’ll be revealing the details a bit at a time going forward.

Xenoblade Chronicles 3 is a new adventure bringing together the worlds of Xenoblade Chronicles and Xenoblade Chronicles 2 to take players into the future. While there is still some time left before the release of the game, I hope you’ll look forward to it.

==

Thanks, Mr. Takahashi!

Xenoblade Chronicles 3 launches this September on Nintendo Switch. Visit the official Xenoblade Chronicles 3 game page for more info.

高桥访谈

As announced in the latest Nintendo Direct video presentation, the RPG adventure Xenoblade ...</blockquote>
苹果自带的翻译：

高桥访谈

正如最新的任天堂Direct视频演示所宣布的，RPG冒险Xenoblade Chronicles 3将于今年9月前往任天堂Switch。为了阐明这一宣布，执行主任Tetsuya Takahashi在即将到来的标题上分享了这一信息，包括一些令人兴奋的小道消息，这些小道消息肯定会引起该系列的粉丝的兴趣。

到你，先生。高桥！

==

大家好，我是MONOLITHSOFT的Tetsuya Takahashi。

《Xenoblade Chronicles 2》发布仅四年多，《Xenoblade Chronicles: Definitive Edition》发布一年半，我们现在为您带来有关MONOLITHSOFT: Xenoblade Chronicles 3最新游戏的消息。顾名思义，这是《Xenoblade Chronicles》系列的第三部。我们目前正在进行最终调整，以确保根据我们从系列中过去条目中学到的一切，创建尽可能最好的游戏。

关键的视觉特征是Mechonis的一把破碎的大剑和Urayan Titan的身体，伤口张开。我想每个看到预告片的人都对最后一幕感到惊讶。这个视觉暗示了什么？我还不能透露这一点。我可以告诉你的是，这种视觉效果是在很久以前构思的。更准确地说，我们在Xenoblade Chronicles开发结束和Xenoblade Chronicles 2开发开始之间想出了它。因此，这不是我们最近添加到该系列中的内容。

我们相信，对于那些玩过Xenoblade Chronicles或Xenoblade Chronicles 2的人来说，以及那些将首次玩Xenoblade Chronicles游戏的人来说，这个游戏都会令人愉快。

这些角色由Masatsugu Saito设计，他还为Xenoblade Chronicles 2设计了角色。虽然我们目前无法透露它们，但Koichi Mugitani创作了一些游戏的关键艺术品。如您所见，熟悉的Xenoblade Chronicles系列的工作人员再次聚集在一起创建这款游戏。

游戏音乐也由过去为该系列做出贡献的艺术家处理。Xenoblade Chronicles 3的音乐由Yasunori Mitsuda、Manami Kiyota、ACE（TOMOri Kudo、CHiCO）、Kenji Hiramatsu和Mariam Abounnasr创作。

这款游戏中的音乐保持了独特的Xenoblade Chronicles触感，同时也面临着新的挑战，即整合基于长笛的旋律作为其主题。长笛实际上是这个游戏中的关键主题之一。预告片中隐藏着各种其他元素和主题，我们将一次透露细节。

Xenoblade Chronicles 3是一场新的冒险，汇集了Xenoblade Chronicles和Xenoblade Chronicles 2的世界，将玩家带入未来。虽然离游戏发布还有一段时间，但我希望你会很期待。

==

谢谢，先生。高桥！

Xenoblade Chronicles 3今年9月在任天堂Switch上发布。有关更多信息，请访问Xenoblade Chronicles 3官方游戏页面。

####  riin  
##### 472#       发表于 2022-2-10 07:56

高桥访谈

As announced in the latest Nintendo Direct video presentation, the RPG adventure Xenoblade Chronicles 3 is heading to Nintendo Switch this September. To shed some light on this announcement, Executive Director Tetsuya Takahashi shared this message on the upcoming title, including some exciting tidbits that’re sure to be of interest to fans of the series.

Over to you, Mr. Takahashi!

==

Hi everyone, this is Tetsuya Takahashi from MONOLITHSOFT.

Just over four years since the release of Xenoblade Chronicles 2 and one and a half years since the release of Xenoblade Chronicles: Definitive Edition, we now bring to you news regarding the latest game from MONOLITHSOFT: Xenoblade Chronicles 3. As the name indicates, it’s the third installment in the Xenoblade Chronicles series. We are currently making final adjustments to ensure we create the best game possible based on everything we’ve learned from the past entries in the series.

The key visual features a broken great sword of Mechonis and the body of the Urayan Titan with a gaping wound. I imagine everyone who saw the trailer was quite surprised by the final scene. What is this visual hinting at? I can’t reveal that just yet. What I can tell you is that this visual was conceived quite some time ago. More precisely speaking, we came up with it sometime between the end of development of Xenoblade Chronicles and the beginning of development of Xenoblade Chronicles 2. So, it’s not something we recently added to the series.

We believe the game will be enjoyable for both those who’ve played Xenoblade Chronicles or Xenoblade Chronicles 2, as well as those who will be playing a Xenoblade Chronicles game for the first time.

The characters were designed by Masatsugu Saito, who also designed the characters for Xenoblade Chronicles 2. While we can’t reveal them at this time, Koichi Mugitani created some of the game’s key artwork. As you can see, familiar staff members with the Xenoblade Chronicles series have once again come together to create this game.

The game music was also handled by artists who’ve contributed to the series in the past. The music for Xenoblade Chronicles 3 was composed by Yasunori Mitsuda, Manami Kiyota, ACE (TOMOri Kudo, CHiCO), Kenji Hiramatsu and Mariam Abounnasr.

The music in this game maintains the unique Xenoblade Chronicles touch while also taking on a new challenge, namely that of integrating a flute-based melody as its motif. The flute is actually one of the key themes in this game. A variety of other elements and themes are hidden in the trailer andwe’ll be revealing the details a bit at a time going forward.

Xenoblade Chronicles 3 is a new adventure bringing together the worlds of Xenoblade Chronicles and Xenoblade Chronicles 2 to take players into the future. While there is still some time left before the release of the game, I hope you’ll look forward to it.

==

Thanks, Mr. Takahashi!

Xenoblade Chronicles 3 launches this September on Nintendo Switch. Visit the official Xenoblade Chronicles 3 game page for more info.

####  5353  
##### 702#       发表于 2022-2-10 09:11

《异度神剑3》官网公布了6名主要角色背景介绍，游戏将于今年9月推出。正如预告开头所言“为生而战，为战而生”一般，本作以“命”为主题，将所属不同的六名士兵编织到一起汇聚成一个波澜壮阔的故事！

“克维斯”阵营：

诺亚（CV:新井良平）：本作主人公，不仅是一名士兵也是在战场上为殒命者吊唁的送葬人。看似身材纤细但却有着很强的体能，深受同伴们的信赖。作为送葬人看到如此多的生命萧然逝去，进而对这个世界产生了质疑。

岚茨（CV:田边幸辅）：诺亚的同伴，以坚强的身躯守护着伙伴。

尤尼（CV:潘惠美）：是诺亚和岚茨的青梅竹马，毒舌且性格上有些粗犷，擅长使用恢复术。

“阿古努斯”阵营：

弥奥（CV:津田美波）：本作女主人公，“阿古努斯”的士兵同时也是送葬人。为人善良，在同伴之间有着很高的人望。和诺亚一样因为特殊的职务使得自己对生命展开了重新的思考。

泰翁：弥奥一起行动的同伴，思维敏捷、洞察力高的战术家。

塞纳：弥奥的同伴，看似柔弱却是个让人无法想象的怪力之人。

*****

####  Piano-Forest  
##### 754#         楼主| 发表于 2022-2-10 09:33

[https://m.weibo.cn/1622008051/4735254273461262](https://m.weibo.cn/1622008051/4735254273461262)

《异度神剑》系列总监督 高桥哲哉 寄语：

《异度神剑2》发售大约4年、《异度神剑 决定版》发售大约1年版，今天我为大家带来了Monolith Soft的最新作品《异度神剑3》。正如游戏名一般、本作是《异度神剑》系列的第三作，目前开发工作已经进入最后的调整阶段，争取让它成为系列的集大成之作。

在主视觉图中的是折断的机神大剑与胴体被刺穿的英维迪亚巨神兽，观看视频的各位想必都被最后的这个镜头所震惊了吧。

这个视觉图代表了什么意思呢？

这一点我们暂时不能公开，其实这个视觉图在《异度神剑》开发结束之后、在开始开发《异度神剑2》之前就已经早早构思好了。

所以新作并不会让人感到违和，不管是玩过一代的玩家还是玩过二代的玩家、亦或者是刚开始接触《异度神剑》系列的玩家都能够享受本作的内容。

角色设计由2代的角色设计齋藤将嗣继续担任，此外，虽然目前还不能公布，但主要的美术工作由麦谷興一等《异度神剑》系列的原班人马负责。

要说亲切感的话还得提一下音乐，《异度神剑3》得音乐由光田康典、清田愛未、ACE工藤ともり、CHiCO、平松建治、マリアム・アボンナサー这6名作曲家参与了配乐工作。

本次的乐曲将保持《异度神剑》系列特色的同时，以用笛子吹奏旋律这一题材进行了新的挑战。这支笛子也是本作非常重要的主题之一，在视频中除了笛子以外也有其他的要素与主题，具体细节我们将在今后公布。

《异度神剑3》是连结了《异度神剑》与《异度神剑2》这两个世界、向着未来进发的新故事，离发售还有一段时间，请大家期待！
<img src="https://p.sda1.dev/4/d55d4045111ee4158b4ee14172dd1275/20220210_093327.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">

异度神剑3

预定发售日：2022年9月
<strong>支持中文：繁体中文和简体中文</strong>

以一望无际的辽阔原野与无缝战斗系统为特色的RPG《异度神剑》系列，其最新作《异度神剑3》预定于2022年9月发售。

分别隶属于两个敌对国家"科维斯"和"安格努斯"的6位少年少女，即将展开一场以"生命"为主轴的故事。

故事的舞台"艾欧尼翁"有着壮阔的自然环境、巨大的原生生物，以及用来当作军队据点的巨型移动兵器"铁巨神"。

这是一个全新的故事，连结了《异度神剑》与《异度神剑2》两个世界的未来。敬请期待后续资讯

今回の脚本作業は、最初に監督から濃密なプロットが提示され、自分と兵頭一歩さんで半分ずつ執筆しました。僕が偶数話、兵頭さんが奇数話だったように記憶しています。

2代剧本高桥自己也写了一遍的，并且情节是实现给了竹田和兵头详细设计的

对光焰本身的寿命也没任何影响
